Eulogy for the Ceremony: On December 23rd, the twenty-third year of the Republic of China, the Shanghai Municipal Government and other eighty-two public organizations offer this eulogy to the spirit of Mr. Shi Liangcai: Oh, admirable is our Mr. Shi, highly respected in his hometown, a brilliant talent known to the world, blessed by heaven. From his youth, he embraced learning, his reputation soaring through the schools. His character and judgment surpassed others. Elders of the time eagerly sought his guidance, anticipating his great potential, and showing him their appreciation. He governed with innovation, nurturing talent. Like a gentle spring breeze, he opened minds and expanded horizons. He was diligent in public service, studying diligently to understand things, exploring principles and seeking origins. With his outstanding talent and insightful vision, he systematized and regulated. Initially, he tried his hand as a traveling merchant, using strategies that ensured success. Utilizing his spare time, he articulated policies on salt and iron, toiling through waves and boiling the sea, benefiting the people's livelihoods. During the recovery of China, every accomplishment, great or small, was achieved through his efforts, his dedication. Wherever the banners and flags reached, no obstacle remained unconquered. After the success, he stepped down, retiring from public office. He embraced hardship and shouldered great responsibilities, responding to changes. With foresight and broad vision, he advocated for goodness. He guided those who were lost. Truly, he was a beacon, becoming prosperous through his efforts. His contributions to the party and the nation were far-reaching, his fame spreading throughout the world. His influence extended everywhere, turning heaven and earth. His grand house was vast, its roof majestic. He cultivated with his heart and blood, focusing on nurturing life. He gathered to distribute, feeling the thirst and hunger of others as his own. He opened granaries and distributed grain, widely practicing benevolence. Nurturing talent was his priority, followed by collecting books. He watered and planted, diligently promoting the people's wisdom. His recommendations were numerous, his reputation growing daily. He remained serene and unchanged, with a clear mind in his simplicity. Occasionally, he offered suggestions, analyzing the subtle and nuanced, resolving conflicts decisively. In crowded gatherings, one word from him would settle matters. In large assemblies, people would hold their breath. Amidst the grand scenery of the mountains, he was a true spirit. The yin符 and the I Ching, he knew the signs of things to come. During the Northeast Incident, when the border troubles suddenly arose, he widened his eyes in anger, striving to suppress the rebellion. The golden goblet was broken, the vast deserts were vast, the jade璧 had shattered, and the brave warriors had no home. He came to comfort and console them, boosting morale. He provided support and assistance, delivering grain. He retained a bit of righteousness, to correct the declining customs. His passionate heart, like Lingwei's crane returning, was still there. He planned for commerce, holding a cup in the apricot grove, navigating the seas. He sat surrounded by a city of books, rivaling the Langhuan Library. He circulated currency, gathering it from the nine treasuries. All these initiatives were met with widespread approval, with countless people looking to him as a role model. But in this unfortunate year, like owls destroying a nest, he faced disaster. He was buried with his cart. He carried his resentment on his back. Dark clouds filled the sky, and the wind suddenly rose. The river's waves soared, and the wild fragrance withered on the ground. At this time, he transformed and ascended to heaven, riding high in a cloud chariot, assisted by a pair of dragons. May he not close his eyes, and look down upon this world of filth. Across the vast seas, everyone weeps for him. With orchid nectar and cassia wine, we express our grief and sorrow. Our feelings reach the gates of heaven. May his soul return! Alas, alas, alas! Accept this offering.

Chen Zhaoying Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday

Discusses the Growing Development of Party Affairs in Fujian Province

Salt Administration Reform Commission May Be Established Next Spring

Chen Zhaoying, Central Committee member and Special Commissioner of Party Affairs for Fujian Province, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning at 7:25 AM, taking an overnight train from Beijing. After getting off the train, he went to his hotel to rest. He is scheduled to stay in Shanghai for two or three days before returning to his hometown of Pujiang County in Zhejiang Province to organize winter relief efforts. A Xin Xin News Agency reporter interviewed Mr. Chen at his residence yesterday, and the details of the conversation are as follows:

Party Affairs in Fujian Province: According to Mr. Chen, he was sent to Fujian Province to reorganize the province's party affairs and has been working for several months. The work carried out in these months has focused on training party members on the party's intentions and concentrating their thoughts. At the same time, public schools have been established in various counties throughout the province to train the public, ensuring they have pure intentions. The development of party affairs in Fujian Province is improving daily, and preparations for recruiting party members will soon begin. In the future, efforts will be made to ensure that the public in every county, village, and town can adhere to the spirit of the party, so that talents from all regions can be gathered.

Suppression of Banditry: The banditry in Fujian Province was originally rampant, but after the army's thorough suppression efforts, it has gradually been eradicated. Currently, in the border counties, there are still some scattered remnants of bandits hiding, but with their old nests destroyed and losing their support, they are powerless. It is expected that all the bandits will be eliminated soon. The political situation in Fujian Province has become stable, and various construction projects are making significant progress. In terms of finance, after the financial authorities made efforts to reorganize, revenue and expenditure are roughly balanced. This year, several new banks have been established in Fujian Province, which have greatly benefited the province's finances by circulating throughout the province.

Implementation of Salt Law: The Xin Xin News Agency reporter then inquired about the process of proposing the implementation of the salt law at the Fifth Plenary Session. According to Mr. Chen, the new salt law was promulgated three years ago, but due to various obstacles, it has not been implemented. Therefore, it was brought up for discussion at the Fifth Plenary Session and approved by the assembly. The Executive Yuan will organize a Political Reform Commission to prepare for the implementation of the salt law. The commission will be established no later than January 20th of next year. Salt is a necessary commodity for the people, and it has a significant impact on their livelihoods. Currently, the price of salt is high, which greatly affects people's food. Therefore, the mission of the Salt Administration Reform Commission is to (1) reorganize salt affairs and increase salt production, and (2) after taxing salt fields, it can be circulated throughout the country. Thus, the accumulated abuses of salt affairs over the years can be eliminated, and the salt law can be implemented soon.

French Consul-General Warns Subordinates Against Accepting Gifts

Mr. Meili'ai, the French Consul-General stationed in Shanghai, aware that in the past, during holidays such as Christmas and New Year's, citizens of this concession would prepare gifts and present them to French Consul-General and the Shanghai Municipal Council police and other public officials. This behavior, according to French law, there is an infringement, so Mr. Meili'ai cautiously warned subordinates that all public officials in this concession must not accept any gifts in order to maintain integrity. At the same time, citizens of this concession were notified not to send gifts.

Local Coordination Council Rescue Team Continues Work in Jiangxi

This summer, the Shanghai Local Coordination Council, recognizing the severity of the disaster and the prevalence of epidemics in the recovered bandit areas of Jiangxi Province, and the urgent need for rescue among the compatriots in the disaster areas, organized a rescue team led by Dr. Pang Jingzhou, a member of the council, in July. They led a team of doctors and nurses to Guangchang Station and other places in Jiangxi Province to work, providing medical treatment and medicine. For four months, they treated over 41,290 disaster victims, with excellent results. They received awards from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, as well as plaques and silver shields from various military units and public organizations, in large numbers. Last month, the council, due to the scheduled work period nearing completion, telegraphed the team to end their work and return to Shanghai. At that time, many places telegraphed to request they stay, but due to time constraints, they could not fulfill the requests to remain in Jiangxi. Recently, they received another telegram from Chairman Chiang and invitations from various local organizations in Jiangxi Province, and now, under the guidance of Dr. Pang, they will continue to work in Jiangxi Province. It is reported that preparations have been completed, and Dr. Pang Gongzhe, Yang Dingguo, and Han Baojiu, as well as nurses Wang Yongling and Zhang Zhijie, will take a large batch of medicines on the Xiyi ship on the 18th evening. On the 18th at noon, members Huang Yanpei, Jiang Wenyu, and others held a farewell banquet for the team members at the council's office to express their appreciation.

Songpu Steamer Freed from Shoal Yesterday

The Songpu steamer, belonging to the Sanbei Company, has been stranded near Wuhu for more than a week. Due to the falling river level, the Songpu steamer had a deeper draft and could not be rescued at the time. Later, the Fuyang steamer and iron barges arrived at the Songpu boat to unload its cargo. Finally, coal was burned in the barges. Until yesterday morning, during high tide, the Songpu could move. The shipowner then opened the engine full power and managed to get out of the shoal. It then went to Pangtzechi to moor. Yesterday afternoon, the company received a telegram from the Songpu shipowner stating that the Songpu's coal and cargo had been completely unloaded, leaving only 300 sacks. At 6:00 AM on the 22nd, the ship was able to escape danger on its own and is now anchored at the lower end of Bangziji. It is now loading coal and will transfer the Fuyang's cargo back onto the ship, and then head to Hankou.

Lian'an Maoli Steamship Company Business Competition Dispute Escalates

Navigation Administration Bureau Thoroughly Investigates Price War

Maoli Steamship Company Asks for Assistance from All Sectors

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, the ships of the Lian'an Shipping Bureau in this city operate on the Shanghai-Taiwan route, sailing according to schedule every week, and the business is developing well. Recently, in order to compete with the Maoli Company, the company abandoned the original Wednesday schedule of the Chuanshan ship and changed it to Thursday, sailing on the same schedule as the Maoli ship of the Maoli Company, causing a major dispute between the two sides. The Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Communications specially ordered a thorough investigation, and the Maoli Steamship Company requested assistance from all sectors to maintain the navigation industry and benefit navigation. The details learned by the Xin Xin News Agency reporter are as follows:

Navigation Administration Bureau Thoroughly Investigates: The Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Communications issued an order to the Maoli Steamship Company yesterday, stating that according to the Lian'an Shipping Company's report, the company was formed four years ago by the Zhoushan Steamship Company, Ping'an Steamship Company, Chuanshan Steamship Company, Daxing Shipping Company, Yili Steamship Company, and Taizhou Xinjihang Shipping Company, which operate on the Shanghai-Taiwan route. In the past, due to business relations, the competition was fierce, and the losses were huge, almost unsustainable. Fortunately, the ministry sent personnel to guide them, and the Shanghai Shipping Association tried its best to mediate, and the company was established to operate jointly and cooperate thoroughly, reporting to the ministry for record, in order to prolong their survival. However, after four years of cooperation, the losses have increased daily, and the reason is that the industry does not understand, and small-tonnage ships often insert themselves to sail, engaging in price wars. For example, the Maoli, an inland port shallow-water ship sailing on the Shanghai-Shazhou route, inserted itself into the market, recklessly cutting freight and passenger prices, which has not stopped to this day. Recalling the difficulty of creating the bureau, it is endless to describe. However, in China's shipping industry, such thorough cooperation is still an innovation. Looking at the other lines, there is no follow-up. To set an example for shipping industry cooperation, every time I remember the kindness of the ministry and the association, I can't forget it. After the cooperation, due to the lack of guarantees, allowing other ships to insert themselves and mess things up, the losses will lead to bankruptcy, which was unexpected at the beginning. Therefore, some members feel that they are bound by cooperation and are exhausted. They believe that individual struggle is better than cooperation. However, at a time when the country is advocating cooperation, if the bureau collapses, it may have an impact and become an obstacle to future cooperation. They are worried and do not know what to do. They believe that shipping cooperation is the only way to save the dying shipping industry. The bureau is guiding and promoting future cooperation, and will certainly try to help the cooperation that has been established and is about to collapse. Therefore, they appeal to the bureau to investigate and verify, and order the Maoli ship not to engage in price competition during the design cooperation period, and strictly supervise it. The future of cooperation depends on this, and it is not just the bureau that can be preserved. According to this investigation, if there is a price war during the cooperation preparation period, it should be strictly prohibited. What is the actual situation? Please reply in detail for verification. (Omitted below)

Maoli Calls for Assistance: After receiving the instructions from the Navigation Administration Bureau, the Maoli Steamship Company immediately reported the process to the bureau and requested assistance from all sectors of the city. The original text reads, (omitted above) The Maoli ship of our company has been sailing on the Shanghai-Taiwan line for more than a year, with accurate schedules and convenient for merchants and travelers. Unexpectedly, Lian'an Shipping Company, a competitor on the same route, wants to dominate the line and does not allow a third party to intervene. Relying on its large fleet and abundant resources (Zhoushan, Daxing, Chuanshan, Dahua, and Taizhou), it is determined to manipulate the market as it pleases. Therefore, based on its local practices, although it knows that it cannot order the Maoli to stop sailing or force merchants to stop loading, it actually sent the Chuanshan ship to abandon the original Wednesday schedule, secretly reducing the fares, and sailing on the same schedule as the Maoli on Thursday. It is clear that it is intentionally disrupting business, making it difficult for Maoli to retreat, and achieving its goal of monopolizing the market. It does not consider that shipping companies should maintain each other when they are bankrupt, and how can they engage in internal strife? According to the company, the design of cooperation does not allow for further destruction. They have assumed considerable responsibility. It is the winter prevention season. If they cannot bear it, the traffic and travelers will be greatly affected. (Omitted below)

Hu Die's Contract Termination Case with China South Chemicals

The third trial ends... Hu Die still loses the lawsuit

Hu Die's appeal in the contract termination case with China South Chemicals to the Supreme Court has ended with the third trial, and Hu Die still lost the lawsuit. The full text of the Supreme Court's judgment is recorded below. Supreme Court Civil Judgment No. 1092 of the 23rd year. Appellant Hu Die, litigation agents Feng Xizui and Qin Liankui, appellee China South Chemical Industry Cooperative, legal representative Xu Gongming, litigation agents Zhang Shizhao and Peng Yuanxun. The appellant appealed the second instance judgment of the Third Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court on April 17, 23rd year of the Republic of China, regarding the confirmation of the non-existence of the contract between the parties. This court's judgment is as follows: Main text: The appeal is dismissed. The costs of the third instance litigation shall be borne by the appellant. Reason: In this case, the appellant agreed with the appellee on June 4, 21st year of the Republic of China that the appellant's name and portrait would be used as trademarks for various cosmetics manufactured by the appellant. Article 9 of the contract states that the cosmetics using Party B's name and portrait as trademarks must be produced by Party A successively within the shortest period of time from the date of signing this contract. If there is no product after one year, this contract will be invalidated. According to the interpretation of the meaning of the text, the so-called "no product after one year" refers to no product within one year. It cannot be said that the appellee did not produce all kinds of cosmetics within one year, and the appellant can claim to terminate the contract. Moreover, Article 11 of the contract stipulates that the operation of several kinds of cosmetics that have been produced may be stopped midway, so it is even more obvious that the cosmetics cannot be regarded as the reason for terminating the contract if they have not been produced all together. The appellant said that the explanation of this article must be that all products must be produced before it can be considered proper. Secondly, although the appellee had disputes with the Family Industry Cooperative due to this trademark, and the business was hindered, it has already produced tooth powder with the appellant's portrait within the agreed period. The court hearing the facts has reviewed and confirmed that the batch of wholesale accounts and Bao Wen Printing Bureau delivery accounts are true, and it cannot be disputed by empty words. Also, Article 5 of the contract stipulates that Party A's business situation should be reported to Party B on a monthly basis. However, this regular report is only for the appellant to know the business situation and is only a procedure for the implementation of the contract, not the content of the contract. Therefore, regardless of whether the appellee fulfills the contract or not, there is no question of termination of the contract. Moreover, the appellant can go to check according to the contract, so it will not suffer any kind of damage, and there is no reason to claim termination of the contract. As for the appellant's claim in appealing to this court that there is a reason to revoke the expression of intent in Article 88 of the Civil Code, it is obviously contrary to the legal precedent that no new facts can be claimed in the third instance, and it is not acceptable, let alone discussed.

Based on the above conclusion, the appeal in this case is unreasonable. According to Article 440, Article 415, and Article 81 of the Civil Procedure Law, the judgment is as stated in the main text.

Brave Bodyguard of Xiekang Qianzhuang Valiantly Kills a Thief

Three Thieves Flee in Terror Without Stealing Anything

Gatekeeper Shot and Injured While Apprehending Thief

| Bodyguard Slightly Injured While Pursuing Other Thieves |

At 8:50 yesterday morning, four bandits suddenly appeared at No. 35 Xuyi Lane, Beijing Road and Henan Road, the Xiekang Qianzhuang, and attempted to rob the business while concealing three handguns. One bandit stood guard at the back door, while the other three bandits barged in. One bandit stood in the parlor, and the other two bandits drew their guns and broke into the accounting room, demanding silence. Just as they were about to begin robbing, the qianzhuang's bodyguard, a Tianjin native surnamed Wang, noticed the bandit standing in the parlor. Without making a sound, he drew his gun and opened fire on the bandit. The bandit was hit in a vital spot and immediately fell to the ground and died. The other two bandits in the accounting room heard the alarm and realized that things were not going well. Without robbing anything, they hurried out of the front door, where they encountered the gatekeeper of No. 32 Lane. Fearing an attack, they opened fire first, hitting the gatekeeper in the head and knocking him to the ground. The two bandits took advantage of this time to flee without a trace. However, after the bodyguard Wang shot and killed one bandit, he was deeply afraid that the two bandits in the inner room would escape from the back door, so he quietly went out of the back door to wait. Unexpectedly, the bandit guarding at the back door heard the gunshots and ran away first. Unexpectedly, the two bandits escaped from the front door, where they encountered the gatekeeper of No. 2 Lane at the entrance of the lane. They opened fire and wounded the gatekeeper. The bodyguard was also slightly injured. After the incident, the general patrol room received a report and immediately sent Chinese and Western detectives to search for the escaped bandits, but they were nowhere to be found. They sent the bandit's body to the forensics office on Fielun Road for an autopsy and sent the wounded gatekeeper and others to the hospital for treatment. It is said that the gatekeeper's injuries are quite serious.

Rickshaw Puller Dashing Forward

Collides with Stone and Dies

| For the Price of Two Small Silver Coins |

At 2:30 pm yesterday, a rickshaw carrying a passenger was traveling east along Xuejiabang Road, Xinjiekou, Nanshi. Unexpectedly, the passenger urged the rickshaw puller to speed up. The rickshaw puller exerted himself, but suddenly lost control and fell on a stone. The passenger also fell over. The passenger got up and was about to question the rickshaw puller, but saw that the rickshaw puller's face was broken, bleeding, and barely breathing. He was lying on the ground unable to get up. He hurriedly took out two coins and threw them at the rickshaw puller, and then hurried away. At the same time, passers-by saw the situation and all tried to save the man's life, not bothering to care about the passenger's escape. When the patrol police heard the news and rushed to the scene, one man was already gone and the other had died. The patrol police reported to the Dongjiadu Police Station. The deceased's family had received the news and came to guard the body, waiting for a legal examination and preparing a coffin for burial. According to the family members, the deceased was only thirty-nine years old, from Haizhou. There was a wife and a young son at home, who all depended on the deceased for support. Now that he had died suddenly, how would they live? After speaking, she wept sadly, and the onlookers all sighed with regret.

Deceiving Women with Weak Wills

Performing Indiscriminate Incisions, Causing Bleeding and Death

Ding A'ren from Haimen used to work at the mint and lived at No. 268 Zhongshan Road. On the 15th of this month, Ding went to work at the factory. Suddenly, an itinerant doctor Wang broke into Ding's house and pointed out that Ding's wife, Ms. Yu, was suffering from jaundice and needed immediate treatment. If she waited any longer, she would be incurable. He used all kinds of threatening words. Ms. Yu listened and believed him to be true, so she asked Wang to treat her. Unexpectedly, the wound from the incision bled profusely. Wang saw that he had caused trouble and still claimed that it was okay. He pretended to go to get hemostatic medicine and took the opportunity to escape. When Ding finished work in the evening and returned home to inquire, he knew that he had been deceived. He searched for Wang but could not find him. Ding was very frustrated. However, Ms. Yu's palm bled for days and could not be stopped. Due to excessive bleeding, she died at 2:00 pm the day before yesterday. Ding A'ren was filled with grief and indignation. He hired people to search everywhere for Wang, determined to catch Wang. He soon learned that Wang was hiding in the Dayangqiao area, so he went to the address and apprehended Wang, and called the police to detain him in the police station under their jurisdiction for interrogation. A Moment of Error Leads Shop Assistant to Tragic Death by Jumping

Why Be Greedy for Petty Gains?

Such a Tragic Death

Wang Afu, a shop assistant from Shaoxing, a counter friend at Lihe Dyeing Shop at No. 531 Xiwuchang Road, Hongkou, was 24 years old. A customer brought a piece of silk fabric (worth three yuan) to be dyed. However, Wang also had a piece of silk fabric of a similar color to be dyed at the same time, but the material was slightly thinner. At about 9:00 am yesterday, the customer came to pick up the goods. Wang happened to be handling them, and a bad idea suddenly arose in his mind. He handed the customer his own piece of silk fabric. After careful inspection by the customer, he realized that it was not his own thing, and a quarrel broke out. The accountant of the shop came out to mediate, and finally the customer's raw materials were handed over, and the matter was settled. The matter was reported to the manager, who believed that Wang's actions had damaged the reputation of the shop. He immediately summoned the person who introduced him to come and planned to dismiss Wang. Wang, upon hearing the news, was ashamed to face others and suddenly had the idea of ​​dying. He jumped from the third floor, causing his brains to burst and died on the spot. Afterwards, the manager of the shop reported to the police station and used an ambulance to transport the body to Tongren Hospital, and then transferred it to the autopsy.

Transportation University Messenger Instigates Accomplices to Commit Robbery

Two More Thieves Caught in the Shanghai Bank Robbery in Western Shanghai

Stolen Money of Only Two Hundred Yuan Recovered, Rescheduled for Further Interrogation

On the 21st of last month, the Yu Garden Road branch of Shanghai Bank sent staff to transport 5,200 yuan in cash by car to the Savings Office of Jiaotong University at the end of Haig Road in western Shanghai. On the way in Haig Road, a gang of robbers stole all the money. The bank reported to various police agencies to investigate and arrest the stolen goods. Later, the Public Concession Police successively arrested the bandits Zhang Zhilong (30 years old, from Haimen, living at No. 10 Fukang Lane, Daxilu, working in a medicine factory), Huang Yaosheng (31 years old, local, living at No. 4 Zhangjiazhai, Daxilu, working as a car opener), Guan Zuozhou (35 years old, from Haimen, living at No. 11 Dongwangjia Lane, Daxilu, working as a tea and food clerk), Zhu Xueneng (24 years old, from Haimen, living at No. 25 Chenjia Lane, Hongqiao North, working as a messenger at Jiaotong University), Chen Goudi (31 years old, local, living in Changxing Pavilion, Dushenfu Road), Tan Jingen (also known as Gendi, 29 years old, local, living in a bungalow in Hujiazai, Lan Road, Gaolang Bridge, working in Xielong Silk Factory), A Mei (44 years old, local, living in a bungalow in Baziqiao, Zhabei, working in Dongxing Leather Factory), Huang Shuncai (26 years old, from Haimen, living at No. 10 Fukang Lane, Daxilu, working as a rice clerk) and other eight people. It was also found that Zhang Zhilong committed a robbery on October 27 with Gong Guorui's family property at No. 186 Xinzha Road and was escorted to the First Special District Court for interrogation. In addition to sentencing Zhang to seven years in prison, the Shanghai Bank robbery should be under the jurisdiction of the Second Special District Court. The French Police requested the Second Special Court to prepare a document to send detective Yang Yilong to transfer Zhang and other eight thieves to the French Police, and then escorted them to the Second Special District Court for interrogation and detention. The case was investigated by Jin Jiulin, the supervisor of the special agency of the French Police, detectives Zhou Buguang, Zhang Ziying, Qian Yumin, and deputy detective Cai Jinzhang. According to the confessions of the criminals, Gu A'jin (36 years old, from Shaoxing, living at No. 19 Xinle Lane, Mintiniyin Road, working as an inspector on a Wuchang steamship) and Xu A'tao (38 years old, local, living at No. 4 Kainan Road) were arrested, and more than 200 yuan of stolen banknotes were searched out. It was also found that the cause of the case was that Zhu Xueneng, the messenger of Jiaotong University, instigated Zhang Zhilong to collude with the party to commit the robbery. Zhang agreed with the party to wait at the robbery location, and he would signal by taking off his hat and waving it high, intending to commit the robbery. The time has been long. In the first robbery, because they saw foreign soldiers exercising near Haig Road, they saw the car carrying the money passing by, but did not dare to take action. The second time, because the car carrying the money was driving too fast, the bandits could not stop it and did not achieve their purpose. The third time, they learned that the bank would be escorting a large amount of money on November 21, so the bandits planned to order Huang Shuncai and two accomplices who were still at large to carry a load of rice straw each and wait on Haig Road. When the Shanghai Bank car carrying the money arrived, Huang and others would block it with rice straw in front, and the bandits would drive the car carrying the money away to achieve the purpose of dividing the huge amount of money they had robbed. It was also found that the bandits, at 6:30 pm on September 10 of this year, robbed Yao Mushun, the owner of the tiger stove at No. 1632 Xiafei Road, of 400 yuan in cash and gold jewelry, Shanghai Bank passbooks, totaling 537 yuan in stolen goods for distribution. This case was interrogated by Judge Qiu Huanrong in the first criminal court yesterday. The police lawyer Gu Shouxi stated the case and said that the police investigation in this case was not yet completed, and there were still accomplices at large who had not been captured, and only more than 200 yuan of stolen money had been recovered. He requested that the date be changed to two weeks later for detailed investigation of the case, to supplement the arrest of accomplices, and to search for the stolen money. He sued the court for interrogation. The court verified the tickets and briefly questioned the defendants, and then ordered the defendants to be taken back into custody and rescheduled for interrogation on the 28th of this month. The defendants were still taken back into custody.

Zhou Haitao Detained for Interrogation

Wang Yushan, who lives at No. 4 Rendeli, An'najin Road, French Concession, has a private car with license plate number 13078 (Concession Pass). He hires Jiang Mingqing from Tongzhou as a driver. Zhou runs a Chinese car school specializing in teaching car driving technology and serves as the principal. On the afternoon of the 20th of this month, Zhou drove Wang Yushan's car No. 13078 out. When he drove to the front of No. 78 on the road, Qi Derong, the six-year-old only son of the elderly Ningbo resident Qi Liansheng (the child's father is 63 years old this year) living at No. 38 Jinyuli on the road, was following his mother, Ms. Hu, out to buy things. The child was crossing the road from south to north, and at the same time avoiding it, he was knocked down and run over by Zhou's car. Zhou did not stop to rescue him and drove away at full speed. A 107th Chinese constable learned of this and rushed to the scene, but only saw the car number and could not catch up. He reported to the police station and sent the injured child to Renji Hospital. The police lawyer Gu Shouxi stated the case, and prosecuted according to Article 291 of the Criminal Law for negligent homicide. The victim's parents hired Wang Shizong as their agent to file an incidental private prosecution. Interrogated the defendant Zhou Haitao, who confessed that he did not see a child crossing the road in front of the car at the time, and did not know that he had hit and killed the child. The witnesses, including the 107th patrolman Yang Afu and Meng Sizhen, were also summoned for questioning. Judge Qiu Huanrong verified the confession and ordered the defendants to be taken back into custody and rescheduled for further interrogation.

He did not cheat her of money or beat her. It was a false accusation. He requested a clear investigation. The court verified the confession and immediately announced the end of the debate, and scheduled the sentence for the 26th. The defendant was still released on the original bail.

Three Robbers Who Kidnapped Wei Tingrong Resentenced Yesterday After Serving Their Terms

All Three Robbers Denied Participating in the Kidnapping Case

The Judge Instructed That If They Were Indeed Guilty, the Sentence Would Be Increased

Wei Tingrong, the former commander of the Chinese Volunteer Corps of the French Concession, Chinese Director of the French Engineering Bureau, manager of the Sino-French Bank, and native of Ningbo, was kidnapped at 11:00 am on July 24, 1929, i.e., the year of the Republic of China. After finishing work at the Sino-French Bank, he took his two sons home in his private car. He was suddenly kidnapped and taken to the countryside of Pudong, where he was held for ransom. He was held in the bandit's den for a month. Later, the French Police ordered the dispatch of Chinese and Western detectives from the general class to go to the countryside of Pudong with the Public Security Bureau to search. They were able to rescue him and arrest three members of the gang, Zhu Jingcheng, Chen Zhongheng, and Tang Shiliang. After interrogation by the former French Public Concession, the three defendants Zhu, Chen, and Tang were each sentenced to five years of imprisonment and sent to the mainland authorities for interrogation after the expiration of their terms. In August of the 20th year, two more members of the gang, Lv Ruowang (from Shaoxing) and Cai Weicai (from Nanhui), were arrested and sentenced to life imprisonment and 20 years of imprisonment, respectively, after interrogation by the Second Special District Court. The details have been reported in previous reports. The three previously arrested criminals, Zhu Jingcheng, Chen Zhongheng, and Tang Shiliang, have now completed their original five-year prison terms. The Second Special District Prison has prepared a document to transfer the three criminals Zhu, Chen, and Tang to the Second Special District Court for review. Yesterday morning at 10:00 am, Judge Qiu Huanrong presided over the interrogation in the first criminal court. The police side was represented by lawyer Gu Shouxi. According to the defendant Zhu Jingcheng, in the 18th year of the Republic of China, he was in Anhui Province, not in Shanghai. He knew nothing about the kidnapping of Wei Tingrong. He was arrested because Cai Weicai implicated him, and the police forced him to confess by torture. He was sentenced to five years of imprisonment by the former French Public Concession. Now that the term has expired, he requests release to redress his grievances. Chen Zhongheng confessed that in the 18th year of the Republic of China, he went to Hangzhou to see the exhibition. He met Lv Ruowang by chance and went to the hotel where Lv lived to ask Lv for the money he owed, but it was not returned. He was then arrested by the Bao Detective and did not know anything about the kidnapping of Wei. The official asked Chen, according to Cai Weicai, you were on the scene as a lookout when Wei was kidnapped. Chen replied that it was a false accusation. Tang Shiliang confessed that in the 18th year of the Republic of China, he was an assistant in the Minsheng Hospital run by Lv Ruowang and did not know about the kidnapping of Wei. His remaining words were vague. After the lawyer hired by Zhu and others stated the case, the court ordered the defendants to be taken back into custody and wait for verification. At this point, the defendants all claimed that our prison terms had expired more than two months ago and we should be released. The official said that if the investigation shows that you did commit the kidnapping, then the prison term will have to be increased, how can it be so cheap? When Zhu and others heard the instruction, they still wanted to argue, but were taken down by the bailiffs and returned to the court.

Holds a Bomb to Intimidate a Foreign Goods Store

After selecting six sections of rayon silk fabric worth 52.10 yuan, he took out a piece of paper from his side with the words "Iron-Blood Anti-Traitor Warning" and placed it on the counter, saying that the store sold inferior goods and that it must be taken to the No. 225 Yongji Lane Office of Fangbang Bridge in the Chinese area to check whether it was inferior goods. He also intimidated the store with a bomb and escaped. The store clerks Jiang Heming, Chen Tingkang, and Chen Xingsheng chased him to the vicinity of Zhoushan Road, frantically blowing their whistles. Police officers have already gone to his home to investigate and found a woman in bed with a child. No other explosives were found, only several cards from his friend, a soldier of the 19th Route Army. The bomb was immersed in water at the inspection office for fear of danger. The judge Xiao Xiefen ordered him to be remanded in custody and rescheduled for investigation.

Health Bureau Reports Results of Tuberculosis Testing in Elementary Schools

Many People React

Treatment Will Be Given Separately Immediately

The Municipal Health Bureau previously conducted tuberculin skin tests in elementary schools, and the Education Bureau designated five schools in South Shanghai, including Danhua, He'an, Songxue, Shangwen, and Weida, to conduct the tests on a selected day. The South Shanghai District Health Office requested Dr. Gao Jinglang from the Red Cross Society to conduct the test. The results were as follows: The total number of students tested at Danhua Elementary School was 426, with 347 reacting and only 79 not reacting, a percentage of 81.4. The total number of students tested at He'an Elementary School was 1,037, with 837 reacting and 200 not reacting, a percentage of 80.7. The total number of students tested at Songxue Elementary School was 197, with 156 reacting and 41 not reacting, a percentage of 70.18. The institute was extremely surprised by the high percentage of reactions in the test results, which shows the severity of the spread of germs. Nurses have now been dispatched to monitor the boys who reacted, and the parents of each student have been notified to pay attention and seek medical treatment as soon as possible. The institute will also dispatch doctors to examine the students who reacted with X-rays to determine the symptoms and then treat them separately.

New members who have recently passed can collect their badges at the venue and pay the membership fee of two yuan. The meeting will begin at 5:00 p.m., followed by dinner after the meeting.

Meeting Order (1) Ring the bell to start the meeting; (2) Elect two chairpersons for the meeting (the presidium consists of five people, three of whom have already been elected by the executive and supervisory committees in accordance with the rules); (3) Pay the highest respect to the Party and National Flag and the portrait of the Premier; (4) The chairperson respectfully reads the Premier's will; (5) Three minutes of silence; (6) The chairperson delivers a speech; (7) Representatives of Party and government agencies deliver instructions; (8) Report and discuss association affairs; (9) Temporary proposals; (10) Dinner and entertainment.

Meeting Staff The meeting staff is as follows: (1) Presidium (those already elected are Yan Duhe, Qian Cangshuo, Jiang Xiangqing); (2) Master of Ceremonies Qian Hua; (3) Secretaries Xu Chihen, Wu Zhongyi; (4) Affairs Jiang Jianhou, Sun Daosheng. Screening of Movies Yang Minshi of the National Education Film Promotion Office has specially dispatched someone to the venue to arrange the screening of a valuable sound film, produced by Fox Film Corporation of America, titled "Pursuit," which is exceptionally exciting.

List of Prizes The association previously appointed Sun Daosun, Zhu Ping'an, Jiang Hongjiao, Ma Chonggan, Xu Chihen, Guo Butao, Tang Shichang, Hang Shijun, and Huang Tianpeng to solicit calligraphy and paintings by celebrities and domestic goods. Shanghai Hunting Society Grand Hunt News

First Grand Hunt Returns Successfully

Second Grand Hunt Scheduled to Depart

The Shanghai Hunting Society's first grand hunt in Ningbo returned to Shanghai a few days ago with great success. Yesterday, a general meeting of members was held on the third floor of the Continental Department Store to discuss the second grand hunt and report on the first hunt. The chairman, Liu Jiugao, and the recorder, Weng Wenyi. The chairman briefly stated that although the association obtained a large number of hunted items such as deer, roe deer, pheasants, ducks, etc. during this trip to Qingshui Bridge, Ningbo, the failure to obtain giant beasts was a regret. The reason is that the mountains and forests in the area, such as Tianlong Mountain and Ma'ao, have long been stationed by professional hunters from Fenghua. Giant beasts are sensitive and have long heard the sound of gunfire and avoided entering the deep mountains. At this time, the sea wind was raging, and the valley sounds and pine waves were deafening. Even if there were giant beasts moving, they were hidden and could not be predicted. Therefore, mountain forest hunting must not only understand geography but also choose the right time to avoid failure. There are thousands of acres of paddy fields along the coast in that area, locally known as Taiqiuban. It is surrounded by large rivers and can only be crossed by boat. There are many wild geese and ducks, making it an excellent area for duck hunting, but duck hunting is often done at dusk. This time, we gained a profound lesson from this. Among the companions was Zhuo Tu

Zhen, a brave young man who does not smoke or drink. We hired a small boat to cross the water when hunting in that area. The wind was tight and the clouds were dense, the mountains were dark and the water was white, and the sounds of geese and ducks crisscrossed the sky. The companions each went to their best spots to shoot, but Shen Tu Zhen's hunting nature was too strong, and he did not think of returning to the team in the dark of night. We then piled up the remaining grass on the ground and lit matches to make a beacon as a signal. After waiting for an hour, we still didn't see him. It was already the beginning of the night, and the cold was pressing. We were even more anxious, thinking that this gentleman had lost his way and had neither a flashlight nor matches to light a fire to signal. The companions were all unable to distinguish directions in the dark. Helplessly, we hired three boatmen to carry flashlights and blow whistles, searching around. At half past ten, we finally brought him back. Indeed, Shen Tu Zhen's face was pale, and he had suffered a lot of fear, hunger, and exhaustion. After this night hunt, we should strictly adhere to the time and meeting place for our companions. For ourselves, we should prepare flashlights, matches, and whistles to avoid accidents. After the report, the second grand hunt was discussed. Mr. Yuan Yang'an proposed to depart by train on the evening of the 28th of this month and return to Shanghai on January 3rd of the 24th year. The hunting area was set as Fuyang as before, which was unanimously approved. Yu Jiexian, the owner of the Hangzhou Erwoxuan, used his 30 years of hunting experience to publish hunting techniques and hunting area selection, all of which were based on practical experience and theories. In addition to Mr. Yu, the new members who joined that day included the famous photographer Mr. Zhang Yuanheng and Mr. Zhou Yingshi. A total of 17 people, including Fang Bingquan, immediately signed up to go to Fuyang. Liu Jiugao, Yuan Yang'an, and Hu Daosheng were designated as members of the Fuyang Preparatory Committee. The registration period was set to end at 12:00 noon on the 27th. The meeting adjourned at 7:30 p.m. In addition, a film of the association's first grand hunt, produced by Weng Wenyi, was shown, collecting all the human and animal competitive activities in nature on the screen, which greatly enhanced the interest. One of them is selected and printed to show the general situation of hunting.

December 22nd

Special Article

A Further Explanation of Mr. Li Fu-sun's Emphasis on Agriculture

By Mu Ou-chu

Recently, Mr. Zhang Jia'ao, General Manager of the Bank of China, advocated a talent-based economy and the development of the interior. Now, Mr. Li Fu-sun, General Manager of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, has also spoken of the importance of agriculture. The attention of these two major bankers in Shanghai to the economic and agricultural development of the interior is not only a guide for the financial community in Shanghai, but also a boon for the economic revival of the entire country. The *Shen Bao* editorial on December 15, "Promoting Mr. Li Fu-sun's Emphasis on Agriculture," argued that the first priority should be ensuring order and stability in rural areas, the second should be regulating rural finance, and the third should be facilitating transportation. Because the central government has strictly ordered provinces to rectify the issue of exorbitant taxes, it was not discussed. The three points raised by *Shen Bao* are indeed prerequisites for revitalizing rural areas. However, how to construct agricultural affairs themselves is even more crucial in relation to emphasizing agriculture. I would like to offer a suggestion for those concerned about rural issues to consider.

In the late Qing Dynasty, the emphasis on agriculture was already heard. Since the revolution, an exclusive ministry of agriculture has been in place for more than twenty years. During these three or four decades, the call for emphasizing agriculture has risen and fallen. However, in recent years, imported agricultural products, such as the rice and wheat needed for people's diets, have not only not decreased but have even increased annually. The fragmentation and decline of the rural economy have reached an irreparable extent. Why is this the case? It is because we rely on empty talk without practical work. Although the nation has established a dedicated agriculture ministry, schools, and agricultural fields, and articles on improving agricultural affairs and revitalizing agriculture have been constantly appearing before our eyes, those who practically go to the countryside to engage in reform are rare. Therefore, for three or four decades, the call to emphasize agriculture has only appeared in the talks of administrative officials and the opinions of contemporary people in newspapers, without achieving the slightest effect. The reason lies in this. Therefore, if we want to lead agriculture to the path of revitalization, it is appropriate to issue less empty talk and seek truth from facts. This is the first point.

One reaps melons from planting melons and beans from planting beans. The quality and yield of agricultural products cannot be deceived by empty talk. Therefore, if the implementation of agricultural policies, the training of agricultural schools, and the dissemination of agricultural fields do not obtain the right people, then not only will there be no good results, but they will also be ridiculed by knowledgeable people and old farmers. Moreover, agricultural affairs are analyzed very finely. Those who plant wheat should not engage in rice cultivation, and those who raise livestock should not engage in forestry. Even within the scope of agriculture, there are things that should not be confused. In the past, our country's agricultural fields grew all kinds of grains and raised all kinds of livestock, but no effect was achieved. Therefore, if we want to manage agriculture in the future, we should recruit specialized talents. If a person has special talent suitable for a certain province, county, or a specific aspect of agriculture, then establish an agricultural field to allow them to experiment and disseminate, and let them preside over it. This is the second point.

The climate varies from place to place, so there is a cotton belt and a wheat belt. The same goes for forests and animal husbandry. Therefore, those who preside over rural areas should seek overall planning, dividing the country's arable land into several regions and formulating specific plans for planting and animal husbandry for implementation. This will not only save talent and money but also achieve greater results. Recently, Chen Gongbo established the Central Agricultural Experiment Institute outside Zhongshan Gate in the capital, Xiaolingwei, opening up thousands of acres of land, gathering agricultural experts from all over the country, and dividing up the research work. Plans of many years have finally been put into practice, which is commendable. Therefore, the third key point in emphasizing agriculture is to plan holistically.

The Rothamsted Research Institute in England has been around for more than 120 years, and the agricultural experiment stations in the United States have been around for 60 or 70 years. Agriculture is a specialized science. With the progress of modern science, its characteristics are constantly changing. How can farming be an exception? The great Soviet botanist Michurin, as an old man of eighty, invented more than 300 new plant species through sixty years of experimentation and research. This shows that agricultural research cannot be effective overnight, and the implementation of agricultural policies also requires persistence. This is the fourth point. If the above four points are all put into practice, can the countryside hope to recover? Not yet. Even if agricultural production increases, and investment is adequate, and it can be self-sufficient, given the strict tariff barriers in various countries today, and the competitive selling and dumping of agricultural products, if there is a bumper harvest, and agricultural prices fall, then farmers will still have no means of survival. Therefore, if our country's industry is not prosperous, even if there is a good harvest, it will still be difficult to achieve real results. The Soviet Union was originally an agricultural country. In recent years, its economy has become increasingly prosperous, which is unmatched by other countries in the world. This is because it has industrialized its agriculture, and the prosperity of industry has helped the development of agriculture. As a result, agriculture has become more prosperous, complementing each other. If both agriculture and industry thrive, then commerce will flourish, national power will be strengthened, and the national economy will also become prosperous. Therefore, emphasizing agriculture should also include emphasizing industry.

Our country's farmers are scattered throughout the country, accounting for the largest majority of the national population. Due to economic constraints and a lack of knowledge and skills, they are always in a passive position. They cannot avoid floods and droughts, and they dare not speak out about exorbitant taxes. In recent years, the impact of the world agricultural panic has made the suffering of farmers increasingly severe. They are left to die in ditches and have nowhere to complain, unlike the industrial and commercial sectors, which can still appeal in a roundabout way. Our country was founded on agriculture, yet the suffering of farmers is so great. Is this not a painful thing? Therefore, if we want to save the countryside today, we must especially rectify domestic governance. If politics are put on the right track, then agriculture will naturally thrive.

Education News

Minister of Education Wang Shijie Discusses Implementing Compulsory Education in 1935

Drafting a Plan Based on the Resolution of the Fifth Plenary Session

Requesting Allocation of a Large Portion of the Boxer Indemnity from the United States, Britain, France, and Belgium

(Nanjing, 22nd) Wang Shijie discussed the Fifth Plenary Session and said that the proposal submitted by the Ministry of Education to popularize compulsory education throughout the country has been resolved and handed over to the Central Standing Committee for handling. The Ministry of Education is now following the spirit of the resolution and drafting a plan for promoting compulsory education in various provinces and cities, which will be promulgated and implemented starting in 1935. At the third joint meeting of various Boxer Indemnity agencies on the afternoon of the 21st, I proposed allocating a large portion of the Boxer Indemnity from the United States, Britain, Belgium, and France for the funding of promoting compulsory education, and a small portion for promoting secondary vocational education and subsidizing the sound research institutes of various universities. Although a general decision has been made, the Boxer Indemnities of various countries have their own special diplomatic relations, so the final decision on the amount still needs to be negotiated with the various Boxer Indemnity agencies. According to a reporter's investigation, the boards of directors of the various Boxer Indemnities have their own diplomatic backgrounds, and the content of the storage and use of the funds is complex and difficult to determine. For example, Zeng Zongchang is in charge of the Sino-Italian Boxer Indemnity, and it is said that the Italian Indemnity has been completely used up. The Sino-Dutch Indemnity has been used as the construction cost of the Jing City Waterway. The actual Boxer Indemnities are those of the United States, Britain, Belgium, and France. On the morning of the 21st, the Ministry of Education first invited the leaders of the Boxer Indemnity agencies of the United States, Britain, Belgium, and France to hold a review meeting at the Ministry of Education to discuss the proposal first. In the afternoon, a third joint meeting was held at the Executive Yuan. Although there was a formal resolution on the proposal of the Ministry of Education, the attendees did not have full power to represent the will of their respective Boxer Indemnity agencies, so it is difficult to reach a definitive conclusion on the resolution.

Joint Meeting of Various Boxer Indemnities Decides to Allocate Funds to Subsidize Compulsory Vocational Schools

The third joint meeting of the boards of directors of the Sino-British, Sino-American, Sino-French, Sino-Belgian, and Sino-Dutch Boxer Indemnities was held in Beijing the day before yesterday. It was decided to allocate funds to subsidize the Ministry of Education's development of compulsory and vocational education throughout the country, among other important proposals. A *Shen Shi* reporter met with a committee member who attended the meeting yesterday and learned the following details:

Attending Representatives: The attendees of this joint meeting included Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei, representatives of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Association Zhu Jiahua and Hang Liwu, representatives of the Sino-American Boxer Indemnity Association Ren Hongjun and Ding Wenjiang, representatives of the Sino-French Boxer Indemnity Association Li Shuhua and Shen Yinmo, representatives of the Sino-Belgian Boxer Indemnity Association Zeng Zongjian and Zhu Shiquan, representatives of the Sino-Dutch Boxer Indemnity Association Shi Ying, etc., chaired by President Wang.

General Assembly Proposals: The general assembly was held in Beijing on the 20th of this month. First, representatives of the various Boxer Indemnity boards of directors reported on (1) the budget and explanation of educational and cultural undertakings for the 22nd year. At that time, the resolutions of the second meeting were also discussed and processed. The general assembly continued on the afternoon of the 21st at 3:00 PM. The Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Education, and the Rural Revitalization Committee all made proposals. It was decided that (1) the annual income and expenditure reports of the various Boxer Indemnity boards of directors should be submitted to the Executive Yuan, (2) the various Boxer Indemnity boards of directors should allocate funds to subsidize the Ministry of Education's development of compulsory and vocational education. The meeting closed yesterday morning, and the results were very satisfactory.

News from the China Educational Film Association

The China Educational Film Association has purchased 30 sets of international educational films and added Chinese subtitles to them. A low rental method has been established for widespread promotion. The films are divided into six groups, and each group charges a rental fee of only 15 yuan per day. They have been screened by the Nanjing Youth Association, Jiaotong University, Wuhan University, Xiamen University, and schools at all levels in Tianjin City, and have been well received. In order to actively promote educational films in Beijing, the association is negotiating with the Beijing authorities to implement educational film measures starting in January next year. In view of the need for educational films in our country, the association has specially sent a letter to the Boxer Indemnity Board of Directors, requesting a subsidy of 150,000 yuan from the interest on the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity, which is allocated to subsidize educational and cultural undertakings, to plan and produce (1) a film on the industrial plan written by Dr. Sun Yat-Sen, (2) films on supplementary teaching materials selected from excellent textbooks, and (5) health films. As soon as the Boxer Indemnity Association approves the subsidy, it can be started. Also, the association believes that although the film industry in our country is gradually developing, most domestic film companies have meager capital and lack talent. From a positive perspective, the government should provide considerable assistance within the possible range. From a negative perspective, the government should also protect and reward it, so that the budding sprouts can grow and thrive. Therefore, based on the resolution of the annual meeting, it is requested that the central government formulate laws and regulations to protect the Chinese film industry, and guarantee the copyright of film scripts. In addition, the film yearbook compiled by the association will be published soon. The price is five yuan, and the pre-order price is only two yuan and eight jiao. The deadline for pre-orders is the end of this month.

Shanghai Branch of the Educational Film Association Seeks to Improve the Fee Collection Method for Educational Films

Schools Find it Inconvenient to Collect Educational Film Fees on Behalf

The Original Method of Collecting Travel Expenses May Be Restored

Since the Shanghai Branch of the China Educational Film Association started screening educational films in various schools every quarter, it has been quite effective. However, this work requires a lot of expenses, so when it was first screened, the association stipulated a method of collecting travel expenses based on the distance of the route, and each school paid the travel expenses each time it was screened to subsidize the expenses. Since the beginning of this semester, the association has applied to the Ministry of Education to collect educational film fees from schools at all levels within the urban area of the city. Primary school students pay two jiao per person, secondary school students pay five jiao per person, and university students pay one yuan per person. Paying the fee once means that they can always watch the educational films screened by the association for free until they graduate. The method is very good, and the burden on students is also light. The association also keeps this fee in custody by a special person and uses it as a fund, without using it. However, since its implementation, many people have been enthusiastic about paying the fee, but many have not paid the fee. The schools that have paid the fee feel it is inconvenient to collect it on their behalf. The Shanghai University Federation and the Shanghai Education Association have first put forward their opinions to improve the fee collection method. It is said that the association is currently discussing whether to restore the original method of collecting travel expenses.

New Chinese Lecturer Arrives at Oxford University

(London Correspondence) Xiu Zhongcheng (Hughes), a director of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Directors, was hired by Oxford University to return to England as a lecturer in Chinese philosophy at the university. He returned to England from China this summer and gave his first lecture at Oxford University last month. The lecture was very popular, with a total of 2,000 students attending. It is said that Mr. Xiu Zhongcheng is quite knowledgeable in Chinese philosophy, especially benefiting from Feng Youlan's *History of Chinese Philosophy* and Gu Dunhuang's *Debates on Ancient History*, which are called masterpieces. This further shows the authority of Feng and Gu among sinologists abroad.

Sixth District Education Association Requests Improvement of the Title for Teachers

Municipal Education Bureau Has Forwarded it to the Municipal Government

Consulting the Ministries of Interior and Education for Instructions

The Sixth District Education Association of this city, in view of the fact that school teachers are mentors of the people's education in the country, and their status is quite respected. Students in schools generally call them "Sir." However, the title of "Sir" is a commonly used verbal title in society. Using it to call school teachers cannot arouse students' respect for teachers and cannot be different from all walks of life, expressing respect for the position of teachers. Therefore, after deliberation by the Board of Directors, it was decided to change the title of "Sir" to "Teacher." It has been submitted to the Education Bureau. It is said that the Education Bureau has forwarded it to the Municipal Government and requested that it be forwarded to the Ministries of Interior and Education for instructions.

Liu Zhi and Others Visit the China Vocational School

Chairman Liu took the stage to give a speech, saying that the reason why the effect of China's education, which has been carried out for decades, is not very significant is that most people only know how to use their brains and do not know how to use their hands. Now, your school advocates the combination of hands and brains, teaching students to study and work at the same time, which is very good. I hope that the teachers and students of your school will work even harder to be a model for vocational schools everywhere, so that Chinese education can be fully vocationalized to save the country and the nation from danger. Then, Chairman Jiang Wenyu gave a thank you speech and dispersed. The details are listed below:

Route: The race route started from the left side of the Zhizhi school gate, went west along Shuidaidian Road, turned left onto Guangzhong Road, then turned left onto Xinshi Road, ran east, crossed the Tudi Temple Bridge, then turned left into Shuidaidian Road, and returned to the right side of the Zhizhi gate. The total distance was three miles.

School Scores: Originally, ten schools participated, but only eight schools attended yesterday. Jianan Affiliated Middle School and Shanghai Affiliated Middle School did not participate due to some reason. The time was 16 minutes and 13.5 seconds.

Wuxi China Sports Federation Football Final, Provincial Xishi vs. Furen To Decide the Winner Again

Draw of 2-2 the Other Day, Replay Today

Yesterday, a letter was received from the Wuxi China Sports Federation, which stated that the content of the Wuxi Secondary School Sports Federation Football Championship published in the sports news column of your newspaper on the 20th of this month, stating that the provincial Xishi won the championship on the 16th, is inconsistent with the facts. It is suspected to be a mistake in the rumor. It was found that the provincial Xishi and Furen competed at that time, and the result was a 2-2 draw. Later, due to slight disorder in the order, the extended competition could not be continued. Now, the Sports Federation has convened an interim representative meeting and decided to refer to the referee Wang Yimin's report. The result was a 1-2 draw and should be rescheduled for a replay. It has now been scheduled to convene both parties at the railway station at 2:00 PM on the 23rd of this month to hold the final again to determine the winner. Please correct it immediately to avoid confusing the audience. Sincerely, Wuxi Secondary School Sports Federation.
