Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

Hopes for Children's Year

— Wang Shouqiu

Now, this year is about to pass! Next year, which is designated as Children's Year, is about to begin! Children, of course, need to be invigorated for this Children's Year, so that it becomes a Children's Year of honor. But how should children proceed? Now I offer a few suggestions.

First: I hope that children can promote domestic products, because next year is not only Children's Year; it is also Student Domestic Goods Year; all Chinese should use domestic products. Therefore, this year we must do it practically and start from you and your family.

Second: You must study hard, because "Saving the country requires studying, studying is saving the country." Children must understand this meaning and must not neglect studying on the pretext of saving the country.

Third: We must practice the New Life Movement, especially paying attention to cleanliness and thrift. For clothes, only cloth clothes are needed, neatly and cleanly dressed; why wear silk and satin?

Children's Year is approaching, and I hope you will be good children in Children's Year.

Little Teacher

— Xidan

Children, do you know who the little teachers are? They are the students in the schools of the Hebei Province Dingxian People's Education Experimental Zone. Because there are too many illiterate people in China, the Hebei Province Dingxian People's Education Experimental Zone called the students in the schools to be teachers of "illiterate villagers," and used their spare time to guide illiterate villagers to read. Although those little teachers are young, they are diligent in service, sincerely and tirelessly teaching villagers to read, and have made many good achievements in promoting people's education in Dingxian, and are still actively promoting it.

Children, what do you think of the facts above? I tell you; this kind of education is indeed an important work for saving the country today, and we can certainly participate in its success, so we must imitate the methods of the little teachers, and call us to go to the countryside to teach ordinary out-of-school children, teach them to read, this is indeed a great mission, but this really wants you to teach people you don't know to read, and at the same time go a long way to teach them to read. As long as our relatives or friends have not received education, or have received very shallow education, then we can implement this kind of beneficial work, isn't this a good way? Finally, I sincerely hope that the children can put it into practice.

Exhortation to Study Song

— Dai Jimin

Exhortation to study, exhortation to study, a man's diligence in learning is heroic. Everything in the world should be done, and nothing in the world is unbreakable. Strive to move forward endlessly, learning is vast, the sea is wide and the sky is high, I sincerely exhort you to study hard.

Exhortation to study, exhortation to study, I advise you not to be just leisurely. Bad habits are formed because of laziness, and time is wasted only because of laziness. Strive to move forward with good morals, the future is vast and full of hope, I sincerely exhort you to study hard.

Exhortation to study, exhortation to study, the teacher is only here to enlighten you. Ten percent of the knowledge is taught by the teacher, and a hundred times the effort is done by yourself. Strive to move forward and shine, knowledge is enriched and fully understood, I sincerely exhort you to study hard.

Getting Up Early

— Bingying

It is winter now, and everyone shouts when the north wind blows on their faces: "It's cold! It's cold!" Rich children are wearing sweaters knitted by their mothers or sisters at this time, and poor children are also wearing cotton-padded jackets added by their dear mothers.

Everyone likes to sleep in a warm quilt, and children often hide in the quilt and refuse to get up; now, many children in school are often late, and only children who don't want to improve are willing to be late! Late is the most shameful noun!

The air is very fresh in the morning. Exercising in the morning is very beneficial to our health, so people who get up early are very healthy. In the morning, our minds are very clear, and it is easiest to remember when reading, so children who get up early have excellent grades. In the morning, the sun rises in the east, the clouds are brilliant, and the birds sing on the branches, the music is beautiful, so people who get up early are very happy. "The plan for the day is in the morning," the morning is the most important time of the day, and we must not waste it!

Children, we must get up early, we must exercise in the morning, we must read in the morning, and do not stay in bed and waste this precious morning; we know that every diligent child gets up very early, we know that every healthy child gets up very early, children, let's all get up early, only lazy cats hide in the quilt in the morning.

The Candy-Selling Boy

— Yangzijiang

I go to school from the corner of Avenue Edward VII and Route Mettemhorst every day, and I also come home from the corner of Avenue Edward VII and Route Mettemhorst every day.

Right below the low wall at that corner, there is a candy-selling boy sitting on the ground. I see him four times a day, and unless it is cloudy or raining, he sits there regularly.

He sells sesame candy. A silk basket is placed on the ground in front of him, with some flattened and some stacked. Sometimes he leisurely shouts:

Do you want to buy sesame candy, three copper coins a piece, three copper coins a piece!

Sometimes he doesn't make a sound, just silently and attentively reading a book. A candy-selling boy who can read and can read so consistently is something I have never seen elsewhere.

What book is he reading? I didn't see clearly, and I was always in a hurry and didn't have time to ask him.

There are out-of-school children everywhere in society, but there are not many who work hard like that candy-selling boy. The motive for writing this article is to hope that many children will learn from the candy-selling boy and increase their interest in reading!

Restraint

— Yian

Children's Science Lecture Series

— Linyin

Another thing we need in our lives is the issue of "movement." The primary event of movement is "roads" (Figure 1). Without roads, people have no way to walk. Even with the tools of movement (cars), there is no way to solve it. With roads, we can use the tools of movement. In cities, we generally use cars for land transportation. There are many types of cars (Figure 2). For long distances, we can also use trains. Human progress, everything is invented according to need. The problem of land movement has been solved, and water movement has also progressed following the land. The invention of ships and the progress to steamships (Figure 3) are still great achievements. We only talk about the improvement of roads and the progress of ships and cars. This issue of movement has already demonstrated human wisdom.

Clearing roads from forests is already a great invention, because mud roads are slippery and uneven, stone roads are easily broken at varying heights, and then building roads with sand, stone, cement, and asphalt makes our walking comfortable. Then, we felt the fatigue of walking, so we invented animal-drawn carts from wheelbarrows. Human life has reached its extreme comfort; however, due to the relationship between speed, we used rickshaws, bicycles, and even trams, cars, and trains. Our ancestors really never dreamed in their dreams that the progress of life had reached the highest level.

In terms of waterways, dugout canoes for crossing rivers were already a great convenience for people. Now, we can use electricity and steam power, and the speed per hour has increased from half a mile to hundreds of miles. Could the people of the early days have imagined this?

But, children! We are now enjoying the happiness inherited from our predecessors. What do we inherit to our descendants?

How to Pay Attention to Hygiene in Winter?

— Linghu Zhao

Little friends, winter and summer are the two seasons that require the most care. Summer epidemics include cholera, vomiting, and diarrhea, while winter ailments are colds and coughs. These seem like minor ailments not worth mentioning, but catching them can be very uncomfortable and even lead to dangerous, incurable conditions.

Little friends, rather than carelessly catching an illness and seeking medical treatment with bitter medicine, wouldn't it be better to pay attention beforehand? The following are some winter hygiene methods:

(1) When coming out of a warm place, avoid exposing your body to the cold immediately, or you will easily catch a cold.

(2) In severely cold weather, open windows and doors less often to avoid cold drafts.

(3) Get up early, walk in a place with fresh air, and do a few minutes of breathing exercises facing the sun.

(4) When thirsty, it is best to drink clean boiled water, without tea leaves.

(5) If someone at home has a cold, their rice bowls, teacups, and chopsticks should be separated to prevent the risk of infection.

(6) More exercise in winter can strengthen the body and increase the skin's resistance. (But be sure not to get cold after exercise, or you will get a severe cold.)

Where Does Gold Come From?

— Ding He

Gold! We all know it. The yellow rings that our parents wear on their fingers are made of gold. But where does gold come from? We don't all know.

Now I'll tell you: Gold is mined from mines. What is mined is not pure gold but is mixed with other metals, called ore. Although sometimes pure gold is mined, it is extremely rare.

There are two ways to make pure gold from ore. The first method is to dissolve the ore or gold sand into a liquid with chemical solutions and then add other chemicals to precipitate the pure gold. Electricity can also be used to separate the pure gold. The second method is to strongly heat and melt the ore or gold sand, and then add other substances to separate the pure gold and impurities. Pure gold is the gold used to make jewelry.

Speaking of this, we should remember the gold-producing areas in our country, such as Chengde, Guishan in Shandong, and Guanxian and Anxian in Sichuan. These are all gold-producing areas, but we rarely mine them. Isn't that a pity?

Steadiness and Luck

— Zhang Nancun

A candy-spinning stall, with a shoulder pole, was resting by the roadside. Hanging from the stall were sugar figures of people, birds, and beasts, decorated with red and green colors, easily attracting the attention of children. As a result, many children surrounded the candy stall, watching.

The candy-stall man held a small wooden stick on his table and spun it around, singing in a melodious voice, "One copper coin to spin for a prize..." He sang for a long time, but many children did not show much interest.

Hai'er saw a candy lion that looked fun, so he bought it for the price. Hai'er's friend, Tan'er, said, "You were fooled. If you could get a prize by spinning for just one copper coin, that would be so cheap. Why pay more money to buy it?"

Tan'er took a fancy to a candy Arhat and put a copper coin on the base of the candy Arhat, hoping to win a prize by spinning. So, he spun it once, twice... until more than ten times, but he never won. The money his mother had given him to buy snacks in his small pocket all ended up in the candy-stall man's pocket.

Tan'er was angry and anxious. He couldn't help but say, "It's really unlucky. I didn't get the candy Arhat, and my snack money is gone. I can't tell Mom about this. I'll just have to go hungry without eating snacks." He looked very distressed.

Hai'er comforted him, saying, "Luck is the seed of failure. Because I remember this saying, I embrace a steady approach. I would rather pay the price to buy it than try to get it cheap by spinning and hoping for luck. These kinds of spinning games are all deception and temptation. From now on, let's ignore them. They won't be able to trick us into being fooled."

Hai'er still had money left in his pocket, so he treated Tan'er to some snacks. Tan'er was very grateful to Hai'er. After that, whenever they encountered lottery-like stalls on the road, they would avoid them as if they were poisonous snakes and fierce beasts, not even daring to look.

Air Pressure Crushes a Tin Can

— Jing'an

Little friends! This is a very interesting experiment. All you need is a basin, filled with cold water, a sealed tin can, and a cork.

First, make a small hole in the middle of the top of the can and pour in a quarter of water. Heat it over a fire to boil, then tightly seal the hole with a cork (if it's not tight, use sealing wax or something else to seal it). Put it into cold water. After about five or six minutes, there will be a scraping sound, and the tin can will suddenly be crushed.

The reason for this is that the inside of the tin can only has a quarter of water. After being boiled, the steam completely drives out all the air inside the can. After sealing the can, only steam is inside. Putting it into a basin of cold water cools the steam, which turns into cold water in about five or six minutes. The tin can becomes a vacuum. We know that air pressure is very high, about fifteen pounds of pressure per square inch. The can cools, and there is nothing inside except a little water. Subject to the pressure of the atmosphere, it is crushed with a scraping sound. The reason why the can is crushed is because of the pressure of the large amount of air outside.

Little Brain Teaser

Five Bowls of Water

— Yan Xinquan

Mr. Shen held five bowls in his hand, placing them one by one on the table. He then scooped a basin of water and poured it evenly into the five bowls. He took out paper and pen and assigned a temperature to each bowl of water. The assigned numbers were seventeen degrees for the first bowl, twenty-one degrees for the second bowl, thirty-four degrees for the third bowl, forty-two degrees for the fourth bowl, and fifty-one degrees for the fifth bowl. He said to Chun Ge, Xia Jie, Qiu Di, and Dong Mei, "Now I ask you, which bowl of water should be mixed with which bowl of water, or is there a simpler method, to make the temperature of these five bowls of water average?"

Chun Ge, Xia Jie, Qiu Di, and Dong Mei all thought hard, thinking for more than ten minutes but could not come up with an answer. They had to ask Mr. Shen to tell them. Mr. Shen said, "This method is very easy. Just pour all five bowls of water with different temperatures into the basin, stir them evenly, and then scoop them back into the bowls. Wouldn't the temperature of the five bowls of water be average then?"

The four children clapped their hands and said, "Ah! That's right, that's right."

Children's Science Game: Cooking an Egg in a Paper Pot

— Jun Peng

Little friends! Are you busy with your studies at school? I think: now there's nothing in nature to look at, isn't that boring? Even if you are busy with your studies, can't you spare one or two hours to do this very strange scientific game? Also, you can cook and eat the egg yourself, and knowing whether it's cooked or not can increase your understanding of many physical principles. Why wouldn't we do this?

The experimental method is extremely simple, and everyone can do it. Just make a pot shape out of drawing paper, tie it to a tripod, pour water into the pot, and add an egg. Then, burn an alcohol lamp underneath. After a few minutes, the water will boil and the egg will be cooked. Hey! Little friends! Do you find this strange? When you burn paper, shouldn't it burn? No, no, it's not like that. This is a matter of physical principles. Let me tell you the reason!

The pots we usually use are made of iron because metals are not easily ignited. Why? Because metals easily conduct heat, and when one part is lit, the heat spreads throughout the entire pot. Wood is the opposite, so paper made of wood fiber cannot be used. So, why can we cook an egg in a paper pot without burning the paper? Because to burn something, that thing must absorb heat. But to burn the paper pot, the contents of the pot must first absorb most of the heat, leaving not enough to burn the paper pot. You see, if we soak paper in water and throw it into the fire, the paper won't burn until the water evaporates. The reason why the paper pot can cook the egg without burning is this principle.

Little friends! This Sunday, use your playtime to do this science game. On one hand, you can increase your scientific knowledge, and on the other hand, you can practice your scientific experimental skills. In this way, you will surely gain many benefits and interests. This is something you must experiment with yourself, so I hope you will experiment as soon as possible!

Women's Garden

Traitors Among the Oppressed

— Jiang Xue

丨丨Miss Chen Xiangjun of Tianjin and her maid, Lianxi丨丨

Women are the most typical of the oppressed and exploited. Housewives can be seen as a microcosm of the oppressed in the whole society. In the family, there are rulers, plunderers, pleasure-seekers, and also the ruled and plundered sufferers. Women丨丨from housewives to maids, belong to the latter category.

Today, we can say that under economic and male dependence, women are all, without exception, oppressed.

However, even though that is said, there are always exceptions. The oppressed can also often be oppressors. These people share some of the plunderers' spoils from their parasitic status, so they forget the enemy and forget their own position. Not only that, but they emulate their enemies, inflicting a kind of oppression and extortion on their companions. The enemy becomes their companion, and the companion becomes their enemy. Without the slightest resentment towards the enemy and without the slightest sympathy towards the companion, they become the enemy's most vicious helpers and henchmen. It is perhaps not too much to say that such people are more hateful than the enemy.

We view incidents such as mothers-in-law oppressing daughters-in-law and housewives abusing maids in this way.

On the 13th, the newspaper reported on the news of Miss Chen Xiangjun of Tianjin and her mother, Chen Xu, abusing their maid. The story is like this: the seven-year-old maid, Lianxi, usually "spread hemp bags" and "sleep on the floor" in a "dark room," eat "leftovers," and is also beaten every day "for reasons unknown," burned on the buttocks with hot tongs, burned on the head with cigarette butts, and stabbed in the face with bone needles.

When we see this news, we inevitably feel stimulated, but when we calm down, we feel that there is really no need to be surprised. There are actually many more things like this! This is just a drop in the ocean. This kind of thing happens in any time and space. Maids and servants are the lowest level of the oppressed. They are oppressed by the oppressed, and they often have to be oppressed by the "traitors" among the oppressed who are several levels above them. As long as this system of exploitation exists, these kinds of things will not only not happen, but it will be impossible to even call them to "happen" less.

However, there is a question and answer in this news that I find very interesting: The judge asked, "Did you beat her because she was naughty?" Lianxi replied, "I'm not naughty. Because I went to the neighbor's, Old Man Huang's, house, Chen Xu went to beat me, and Old Man Huang held me back. Later, Old Man Huang sent me back, Chen Xiangjun blocked my mouth, pressed me down, and Chen Xu beat me with a rattan cane." The implication seems to be that if Lianxi was naughty, she deserved to be beaten. It can be seen that a person who hires a maid, hiring a maid is of course legal, and if the maid is naughty, it is still excusable to hit her. What the law wants to punish is only when the maid is not naughty丨丨to put it more bluntly, does not violate the master's will丨丨and is beaten. But our views seem to be different. We feel that no one should have the right to exploit the labor of others. Hiring a maid should be punished by law.

There are also noteworthy points in the conversation between the judge and Lianxi. The judge asked: 'What does Chen Xu do every day?' Lianxi supplied: 'She doesn't get up until twelve o'clock. After washing her face, she still lies down and sleeps...' Asked: 'What do you do every day?' Answered: 'I get up at seven o'clock every morning to sweep the floor, wipe the table, and light the stove. After Chen Xu finishes eating and goes to sleep, I eat. I eat her leftovers.' Asked: 'What does Chen Ruizhang (i.e., Chen Xiangjun) do?' Provided: 'He learns to act in dramas.' Asked: 'What does Chen Xu do?' Provided: 'She calls for Chen Ruizhang to learn to act in dramas.' We all see it, the life of the oppressor is so corrupt and enjoyable丨丨while the oppressed is so laborious and miserable! Therefore, the oppressors are really the ones who should be oppressed, and the oppressed are the ones who should oppress these demons!

Autobiography of a "Social Person"

— Xian

丨Nora After Leaving Home, In a Corner of Society丨

The editor of Women's Garden knows that I have been in society for several years, so she gave me this topic and asked me to write about my experience. At first, I felt it was very difficult because I was not good at fiction, and if I wrote honestly, it would not be very beautiful. But after thinking carefully, these experiences are all social phenomena. Making these phenomena public as objects for studying women's issues is the duty of every woman.

When I was still in school, I was in heaven丨丨children's heaven. I never thought about families or societies, things outside of heaven. At the same time, my mother died too early, and my family did not give me much of an impression.

From the age of ten, I lived in school. School is separated from the family and not connected to society, so it becomes heaven in the clouds. I lived in heaven for twelve years. Because of economic difficulties in my family, I was forced to enter society. At this time, I was just over twenty years old, my wings were not hard, my feathers were not full, and I was timid and afraid to enter that unfamiliar society. I didn't think about going home either. I hoped that I could enter heaven again, or that someone would come to help me. Who knew that I would be tricked by society and locked in a family?

Since I was unwilling to be locked in a family, I was unwilling to do, unable to do, and simply didn't know how to do things related to the family, such as serving my husband, pleasing my in-laws, and supporting my children. At the same time, he was an author without a job and had not yet become famous, and our life was very difficult. In order to share the responsibility for the family's economy and reduce my husband's pain, I often thought about entering society. But no one sympathized with me or helped me.

Crying, resentment, and hatred could not destroy my desire for "independent life" and "free life"! The "eating someone's food and obeying someone's orders" life that had no reason to obey, I was unwilling to live any longer. During these times, I thanked a sister who liberated me. So I finally entered society.

At first, I taught in my hometown in Hunan. Because of the divorce, I was unduly insulted and despised by the environment丨丨society. I couldn't bear the trampling, so I fled from my hometown to Beiping.

In Beiping, I lived in the home of a relative, waiting for work. Probably it was always my fault that I provoked the relative's wife's unprovoked insults in just three or four days. In reality, I had never loved her husband, and she thought that I丨丨a divorced woman丨丨was born to be trampled on. Before long, I went to a newspaper in T and became a proofreader.

From this time on, I officially entered society. There was not a single acquaintance; all my colleagues were men, except for one woman who was very familiar with them.

The newspaper was a business with some official atmosphere. There were five or six proofreaders, and Mr. W and I were responsible for the two pages of important news.

The atmosphere was tense, or at least, it gave me a lot of new stimulation. The first thing I can't forget is this: Not long after I took office, thanks to the promotion of Mr. Y, the editor-in-chief, I was assigned to be the deputy editor of the supplement. It turned out that the formal editor had been on leave for two or three months, and Ms. X, the other female proofreader, and Mr. G, who edited foreign news, were jointly acting as editor. Mr. G was responsible for reviewing the manuscripts, and Ms. X was responsible for the rest of the affairs. Now that I was the acting editor, and the editor-in-chief had also issued a note (she was privately entrusted), Ms. X was very unhappy. She used the excuse that the editor-in-chief's handling of affairs did not follow the procedures, and that she had not been notified of the handover, so she made a big scene. Originally, in terms of qualifications, she was much older. I had only been there for less than two months; in terms of personal relations, although I was the president's nephew, she and the president were also family friends, plus direct friendship. Moreover, everyone in the newspaper, except the lower-level proofreaders and workers, had known her for a long time, and they often joked and played together. What was the reason for me to get this position in this kind of newspaper?

As Ms. X said: Because the editor-in-chief was biased towards me? According to Mr. Y's explanation, he often saw me writing articles in the supplement, so he recognized my writing. The president had a letter asking him to assign one of the two female employees at will, so he naturally assigned me.

The matter caused embarrassment to both sides, and Mr. Y didn't want to offend Ms. X, so he telegraphed the editor, Mr. C, who was on leave, asking him to come back to work as soon as possible. Mr. C came back soon, and I remained a proofreader. Ms. X and I were reconciled.

The evil consequences have already been sown, and the future troubles are just beginning. When I first entered society, I was naive, simple, and innocent. I didn't know that I should be respectful (formal etiquette) and communicative to my superiors. Ms. X was the opposite: her "political skills" were very high, and she used both active and passive means to deal with me; it seemed that nothing less than this could eliminate the hatred in her heart and avenge the revenge of the previous day.

As luck would have it, once, Mr. W proofread the editor-in-chief's editorial and dropped a paragraph, so the tone of the following text was inconsistent with the previous text. The next day, when the newspaper was printed, the editor-in-chief was furious. He immediately issued a note, deducting five yuan from the salary. He also told us that I would be responsible for proofreading the editorials from now on. Thanks again to Mr. Y's promotion, this resentment was naturally directed at me.

The fatal wound that society gives to women is the arrow of chastity. To suppress women's development and destroy women's rights, all you have to do is groundlessly accuse her of "bad behavior," even if she has the intelligence and talent of Wu Zetian, Empress Dowager Cixi, or Li Qingzhao, she is not worthy of respect. Just because I was more active and didn't pay attention to the inherent virtues of women such as "chaste and gentle"丨丨I liked to talk to male colleagues, or the two or three of us sat and talked quietly, or listened quietly to them discuss international politics, or even sometimes studied problems with a man in the bedroom, etc.丨丨and at the same time didn't know the new skills of "bragging," "acting coy and charming," my crime was judged by public opinion (the so-called public opinion is the public opinion of the masses in the newspaper).

One night, because an outside reporter asked me to record a rather interesting piece of social news for him, he described his experiences in my bedroom. The weather was hot in June, and our small proofreading room in the pigeon-cage-like Chinese-style foreign house was not well ventilated. The large editorial office had more than ten electric lights and more than a dozen people. In order to be comfortable, I often proofread in the bedroom. The bedroom was shared by Ms. X and me, but she proofread the supplement during the day and rarely slept here at night, so it was also very quiet. But although it was a bedroom, it was connected to the studio, and opposite it was the president's office, so it should have been a public place, except when we locked the door to sleep.

Perhaps because the story was told in an interesting place or because I couldn't write a word, we laughed. The laughter reached the ears of the president, making his thick eardrums vibrate in a new way, and his nerves felt uneasy. He immediately ordered the reporter to go to the studio and called me to his office to give me a big lecture, saying that women should be "graceful" and "chaste and gentle." This is the virtue of women.

I accepted the four words "graceful" to some extent. Perhaps I still couldn't get rid of some girlishness, "fidgety" and "not very graceful." I should examine myself and humbly accept the teachings of him丨丨my father's friend丨丨.

But I couldn't help but feel disgusted by the second lesson. Even though the grindstone of life oppressed me, I could only temporarily let me lose my job and find another job.

The matter was very simple: The newspaper held an editorial meeting, and he cancelled my qualification to join the meeting in the meeting place. The other male proofreaders were sitting there, and X You was on leave. What authority and reason did he rely on to insult me like this? I really wanted to ask him on the spot, but who had the courage to support me? At this time I understood. I was so angry that I didn't say a word and walked out. Afterwards, I wanted to deal with him through legal procedures, but I thought: The law cannot protect "my" personality.

I quietly left this newspaper like this.

I failed in society; I knew it wasn't because I lacked ability or courage; it was just that I lacked social awareness and didn't know how to properly place myself in every social environment.

After this, I still struggled in society and lived a very difficult life. What I encountered was that every environment gave me an unexpected new stimulus. I was surprised and I doubted: Did I really do something wrong?

Woman, oh woman! Entering society is like entering prison.

But I am not willing to retreat. I want to be enterprising. I hope to transform this prison into a paradise for people!

Special Group of Nurses

— Qian

Before "January 28th Incident," in a certain neighborhood near Zhabei, there lived a family considered "strange" by the neighbors. It seemed many people lived in this house, but there were neither frail old people nor infants in swaddling clothes, and not a single robust man. Those who entered and exited the house all day were women of varying ages. Although these women usually wore elaborate qipaos and leather shoes, upon closer inspection, one could see differences among them. Those who wore high heels accounted for only one or two tenths of the group. Their hair was always curled, and their faces were painted with red, white, and even black. The "reformed" group, who wore practical, half-sized, all-weather leather shoes, had faces that were yellowish-white, and their hair was either slicked back neatly or unkempt, resembling a pile of scorched yellow straw. Others had not yet rid themselves of their "three thousand worries" and still wore their hair in a bun resembling a teapot handle, hanging on the back of their necks.

What kind of women were these? They were professional women on the front lines of their careers! Their profession was to serve the sick for the wealthy as special nurses, or as they proudly called themselves, Special Nurses. This "strange house" was a kind of trade association-like public house formed by many of them for the convenience of their business. The origin of these special nurses, like that of general nurses, was the church schools and hospitals that came to China along with the imperialist warships. These associations were mostly formed by people who had graduated for some time and were tired of the monotonous hospital life, in order to meet the great demand for special nurses from wealthy patients in Shanghai. Because being a special nurse was not only freer in life, but also the remuneration, when work was busy, was double or three to four times the monthly salary of an ordinary nurse.

Speaking of remuneration, there were original regulations in their profession. They served the sick in day and night shifts, both calculated at five yuan per shift. If they understood English and served foreign patients, it was five taels of silver per shift. As for the work, it also varied in intensity depending on the patient's condition. Generally, it was just to carry out the doctor's orders, take the patient's temperature, check their breathing, count their pulse, administer medication, and occasionally take care of their diet and excretions.

Although these women could obtain considerable comfort and freedom in their material lives through their own labor, their success or failure on the path to marriage could not escape the established laws of society. That is, the young and beautiful ones were snatched away by wealthy patients and ambitious doctors before they could complete their four or five years of arduous apprenticeship. Those who were less attractive or more strong-willed, after a few years of apprenticeship and a few years of professional pursuit, not only had their youth abandoned by the roadside, but also their chances of marriage had long faded with the passing of time.

In fact, it was not impossible for them, aged twenty-seven or eight, or thirty to forty, to get married, but as the saying goes, "too high to reach, too low to accept." The rich and powerful, or modern young men, did not disdain them for being too old, but despised their humble profession and would not favor them. As for those who were about the same age as them and relied on their own labor to earn a living, they were unwilling to stoop so low. In fact, having grown up in such a hypocritical and vain environment, and often entering and leaving the luxurious mansions of the wealthy, they could not get used to the lives of couples who could obtain equal enjoyment through equal labor after marriage. In addition, their feudal consciousness was still very strong, and they still considered it shameful for a woman to marry after thirty. For these complex reasons, they had no choice but to join those who had had problems with marriage, were confined by feudal ideas within their families, and had received hypocritical and anesthetizing education. Those who had resolved not to marry then took this path to make a living, and older women (who accounted for half of their number) spent their entire lives enduring the embarrassing life of washing heads, rubbing feet, wiping feces, and pouring urine for wealthy patients, or even entertaining those wealthy and idle fake patients. Moreover, unfortunately, they had to inevitably witness and send off the coming and going of the grim reaper covered with a black veil. When serving patients with infectious diseases, they were even more at risk of their lives.

On the other hand, these women were not only not enthusiastic about seeking progress in thought and learning, and improving their own status, but also did not understand it. Although this was due to their strong complacency, the biggest reason had to be attributed to the special education they received. Under the slogans of "serving God" and "helping neighbors," hypocritical religious figures exploited them like docile sheep without pay for four or five years. And what knowledge and skills did they give them? Apart from making beds, taking temperatures, dispensing medicine, and taking bedpans for patients, they would not offer much else. However, on invisible gifts, they were very generous in promising them heaven. Therefore, they believed in their consciousness that since they could now support themselves, not only was the problem of this life solved, but there was still happiness waiting for them in the next life. So they became a kind of life that was harmless to others and uncontroversial to the world, and this kind of life often easily flowed into a type of absolute selfishness.

Removing everything on the surface, and adding religious hypocrisy and chains to their inner "sexual" lives, it is undeniable that they were subjected to greater suppression. Therefore, homosexual love was quite common among them, and nine out of ten had a very close female friend. Although they were all nominally friends on the outside, the situation of sharing the same pillow and quilt, being considerate and intimate, and relying on each other far exceeded that of ordinary friends.

Regardless of whether the service of these special nurses is limited to wealthy patients, there is no question that it can become a suitable profession for women. Therefore, I hope that the sisters engaged in this industry will make special efforts to improve the health of their own spirit and body in addition to its economic implications; I also hope that those who are enthusiastic about the women's movement can make efforts to supervise and guide this women's profession.

European Women in the First World War

— Huang Nianzhong

Everyone is preparing for the Second World Massacre, and it is not without meaning to talk about European women in the last madness now that women are about to prepare to say goodbye to their lovers and sons going to war with tears.

After 1914, in every country in Europe, tens of millions of workers, peasants, and students were dragged into the trenches by the slogan of "patriotism", so there were tens of millions of families, tens of millions of women and mothers who were anxious and sad day and night. In the entire four years, the tears that most of them shed for the anxiety of life and the grief for the dead will definitely not be less than the bullets consumed in that era!

But there was also a kind of person who felt some anxiety, that is, many great entrepreneurs felt the lack of labor. Men with labor abilities had all gone to the front lines, and the remaining women became the target of their solution to this anxiety.

In Paris, London, and many large industrial cities, almost all the drivers and ticket sellers of all public vehicles, the service personnel in all industrial fields, and the clerks of all stores were women. Street vendors and porters sometimes also used women. Large cities almost became a world of daughters.

They were very bitter, especially the wives of soldiers. Often, drunken women could be found on the streets, all of whom were strong women who missed the conscripts. Although according to the bourgeoisie, they were abusing freedom after leaving men, had no sense of responsibility, and were willing to fall because they could get conscript family allowances, this argument was obviously wrong. Most of them were willing to indulge in oblivion because of loneliness and because of life.

The plight of women in the lower classes was even greater. Their husbands went to war, and the family expenses and the education of their children had to be borne by themselves. Although there was also some separation pension, it was of no help at all. They had to throw their children into boarding schools in slums, letting them be half-fed and half-starved, while they took over the manufacturing of weapons that would kill their husbands and sons at wages lower than those of men, or manufactured a large number of war-speculation commodities for industrial leaders. At that time, the British government and commercial organizations had a lot of competition in order to win this cheap female labor. Both sides wanted to obtain special wartime convenience or special profits from these helpless working women.

However, in this extraordinary period, working women also gained many valuable experiences. They tested their own abilities, shattered the social prejudice against women's contempt, and exerted the same abilities and knowledge as men in all industrial sectors. In the dangerous munitions factories at that time, the difficult machinery workshops, and all the affairs of complex machinery, it proved that women's inventive talents, adaptation, and enthusiasm surpassed men. No one dared to give a low evaluation of women's social and economic value.

At first, women were not allowed to participate in medical work in England. Many enthusiastic women voluntarily established war hospitals in France and achieved remarkable results. Their excellent results were passed back to their own country, so the officials of their own country immediately employed women in medical affairs. Later, in the garrison hospitals in various parts of London, except for the gatekeepers, from the honorary major doctors to the non-commissioned officer managers were all educated women. In France, helping the victims of Pelgium and northern France, helping the homeless in Alsace and Lorraine, so that tens of thousands of families did not lack clothing, and tens of thousands of children were able to go to school safely, these are all the achievements of French educated women.

In the Great War, working women and educated women tasted a lot of hardship. On the other hand, they also fully exerted their creativity and organizational power. Their 丨丨 especially the success of this kind of test of their own strength by working women, accompanied by the suffering of reality, further promoted their broad unity. The organization of the "National Women's Labor Union" in the United Kingdom, which proposed future occupational insurance and the demand for equal wages for men and women, is a concrete example of this unity.

Perhaps everyone will ask, in this unprecedented turmoil, what do the leisurely bourgeois ladies do?

The cannons could not penetrate their deep boudoirs, and the rough black bread would never reach their lips. Their lives were as comfortable and easy as ever. Occasionally, on the streets of London, you could see some upper-class women wearing khaki volunteer uniforms doing so-called "defense" work. In the safe areas of the battlefield, you may encounter one or two visiting "charitable" noblewomen, but all this is the romantic of their private lives, to borrow Gorky's words, "for the sake of monotony", and has nothing to do with the public.

Secondly, let me mention the gender relations during the European War. From Remarque's books, we can see some sexual chaos of upper-level sergeants, and from Barbusse's books, we can see some failed sexual pursuits of lower-level soldiers. The masterminds of the war isolated tens of thousands of young and strong men and women, but it is generally impossible to make them maintain the mood of a monastery through the abandonment of humanity. Therefore, on the front line, soldiers have three w (Women, Wine, War). For soldiers, the first W also added many secret events of exchanging soldiers' bread. In the rear, romantic stories became the most common phenomenon. All this further reveals the hypocrisy of the so-called monogamy, and at the same time, the treatment of illegitimate children has become the most thorny issue for the party leaders of the warring countries today.

The clouds of war are spreading again today. Women, remember the lessons learned by European women in the First World War!

People Living Under Two Kinds of Hunger

— Benzi

On a Sunday afternoon, I walked past the Great World. Under the wall on its side, there stood a large crowd of people. Out of curiosity, I squeezed in too. It turned out that they were looking at the notice of the Second Special District Court. Its general meaning was: "Rape of a woman under the age of fifteen will be sentenced to seven years of imprisonment; gang rape by two or more people will be sentenced to life imprisonment...to maintain humanity and social morality." After reading it, I immediately thought of the social news of Shen Bao on December 11th: "A fifteen-year-old girl was gang raped by nine young men all night." This notice may be to repeatedly publicize the so-called legal provisions to warn the citizens because of this matter.

This is such a fortunate and pitiful thing! We live in this uneven society, and we are heavily pressed by the boulders of double hunger, so that we cannot even breathe a sigh of relief! This piece of social news clearly explains that, in order to eat, a girl who does not understand the world and whose development is not yet mature is driven by hunger and cold to engage in the prostitution career of a goddess. A group of young people who wanted to vent their wolf-like carnal desires gang raped this underage girl. This is the expression of the impulse of sexual hunger!

In this world economic panic, the storm is impacting every corner of the world. After the turbulent waves of this black tide of panic, the rural areas of our country are extremely poor and bankrupt. The domestic feudal landlords, the bourgeois usurers, and the harsh taxes also explain the good data on the fall of the rural areas! Groups of rural women, in order to escape famine, all ran to the city. They thought that the city was the food place for them to escape hunger, but when they gathered at the crossroads of this city that seemed to have abundant food, their illusions, like the beautiful soap bubbles played by children, soon shattered丨In this way, they began to wander and wander. For two meals of unsatisfied food, they, like the unemployed female laborers in the city, automatically or were seduced into becoming professionals who sold their flesh in nightlife. The deepening of the economic bankruptcy of the rural areas and the increase in the unemployment of female laborers in the cities, the number of prostitutes who sell themselves has increased at a positive proportional high speed!

Everything in the current society is commodified, and the instinctual demands of sexual life have also developed abnormally. On the one hand, there is a relative surplus of women, and on the other hand, a large number of men are living as bachelors. The former is the cause of the latter, and the reason for this strange phenomenon is very simple: in years of widespread depression, the number of unemployed men is increasing day by day, and those with jobs are also living in distress or half-starvation. Where is the extra money to marry a wife? Moreover, the fear of bearing the burden of life after marriage will also make men afraid of marriage. Then, in order to satisfy the demands of their sexual instincts, the only way is to prostitute themselves!

Xin Feng Foreign Firm reported that yesterday (the 21st) the New York stock market was mixed and dull. Purchases were limited to special stocks. The pressure on public utility stocks had dissipated, and the potential of their major stocks had shown some firmness. Automobile stocks were very stable, oil stocks were firm, and railroad stocks had mixed gains and losses. There was little change in small exchange stocks. Chicago wheat trended upward. The daily turnover was 920,000 shares.

Yarn Flower Prices Lowered by Rumors

The yarn market is trending weak, with a sudden drop in prices. Gold prices have fallen by about twenty yuan. Various rumors are circulating in the market, claiming that the equalization tax may be abolished, and that a loan from a certain country has been finalized. At the same time, sales of spot yarn have turned sluggish again. In the afternoon, the market trended downwards, but large holders remained calm and did not move large quantities.

Golden Rooster Gradually Softens: The opening of the spot yarn auction continued the upward trend. Because gold prices closed at a high point the previous day, and American cotton also rose, sentiment was good. There was a lack of sellers in the market. Unexpectedly, by the second and third rounds of bidding, market prices suddenly reversed. Spot yarn sales were not smooth, and gold prices fell below the 1,000 yuan mark. Selling pressure was relatively strong. As a result, prices for all months fell by an average of 1.2 jiao. In the afternoon, rumors resurfaced in the market. The authorities issued another cautious statement, denying any intention to concentrate cash. Various rumors were unfavorable to bullish positions. Market prices fell round by round. As a result, prices for all months fell by 2.6.8.9 jiao. Sold: Tong Kee 700 bales, Geng Feng 4,500 bales, Shen Chang 400 bales, Yi Da 550 bales, Chang Feng 550 bales, Tong He 1,150 bales, Run Kang 2,250 bales, Xinhua 500 bales, De Ji 650 bales. The American Cotton Market is Quite Firm

丨Indian Cotton Trend Also Rising丨

The opening of American cotton yesterday was flat, with market prices rising slightly by one pound. Subsequently, purchases by colleagues and brokers strengthened the market. Sales of cloth are expected to equal two weeks' production. Bullish closures and short selling in January were absorbed by Liverpool and Wall Street. October prices were very firm due to rebalancing and new purchases. Rumors that the government was selling in New Orleans hindered the rise, but colleagues continued to buy. At the close, the market was very firm, with prices for all months rising by one to nine pounds. As a result, spot prices were unchanged, and futures prices rose by two to seven pounds. British spot cotton rose by 2 points, and futures rose by 1 point. Indian cotton rose due to purchases by a few speculators and cotton merchants in the market. Pingguoer rose by 2 rupees, Aomula rose by 3.5 rupees, and Bailuoxi rose by 3 rupees. The original telegram is on the left (dated 21st).

American Cotton Prices Difficult to Rise or Fall Last Week

New York, December 21st: A report on the cotton market for the week states that although the majority of voters support continuing the implementation of the Penghai De case for this cotton season, interest in the cotton market has not increased significantly. Prices rose slightly, followed by selling or closing of positions. With the holidays approaching, the market eventually returned to calmness. Merchants are now awaiting an indication of next year's quotas. Most of the transactions this week were for near-term settlement. Reports of scattered trade from various parts of the country are quite good. General transactions are improving, so sentiment is good, but the interest of speculators is not yet significant. The cotton loan amount is set at 1 jiao and points, so the selling price cannot be considered low. However, when prices are high, cotton farmers may continue to sell publicly stored cotton. It is expected that the market situation will be between not being able to fall and not being able to rise. Prices will likely stabilize at current levels. Only stronger purchases by colleagues can maintain the upward trend. At the same time, the possibility of German goods being exchanged for American cotton seems unlikely, as it conflicts with the general policy of the State Department on international trade.

Grain and Flour Markets Weak but with Restraining Force

Yesterday's flour market, after opening in the morning, the market situation for each month generally showed a stable and unchanged trend. Quotations for foreign wheat were around 1 jiao and 6 fen higher in Chicago, and there were differences of 4 fen in Canada. When prices opened, this month's contracts, due to the approaching settlement date, had more trading and saw some liquidation. Market sentiment had been weak. Afterwards, because both sides were very quiet, and sellers were more balanced, market sentiment turned stable again. By the time the market opened in the afternoon, this month's contracts were being absorbed step by step amid uncertainty due to active spot sales. Market sentiment was weak but stable. Distant months saw strength because factories were not selling and there was continued buying from the interior. Market sentiment was firm, but in the context of quiet trading, this kind of rise and fall was very calm. As a result, the current month was down 2 li and a half, January was up 1 fen, February was up 7 li and a half, March was up 1 fen and 2 li and a half, April was up half a fen, and May was down 2 li and a half.

Spot Wheat Concedes as Buyers Persist

Yesterday's futures wheat market, after opening in the morning and afternoon, the market situation for each month generally showed a stable trend. Quotations for foreign wheat were 1 jiao and 6 fen higher in Chicago, and there were differences of 4 fen above and below in Canada. When prices opened, trading for each month remained quiet. However, as there were fewer sellers, there was a slight rebound. Therefore, each board seemed to tighten. However, trading was very quiet, and this rise and fall felt very dull. As a result, the current month was unchanged, January was up 3 fen, and March was up 1 fen. The spot wheat market had been holding steady for many days, but yesterday, due to customer concessions, asking prices fell by 3 to 4 fen. Dong Xuzhou wheat was offered at 4 yuan, second grade at 3 yuan and 9 jiao and 9 fen, Liuhe Baoying wheat at 3 yuan and 9 jiao and 4 fen, Yangzhou Yaowan wheat at 3 yuan and 9 jiao and 3 fen, Haizhou wheat at 3 yuan and 9 jiao and 6 fen, Bengbu wheat at 3 yuan and 9 jiao and 7 fen, Jiangjiaba wheat at 3 yuan and 9 jiao and 8 fen, and Luohe wheat at 3 yuan and 9 jiao and 2 fen, totaling 12,000 bags, which were taken by Fuxin.

Chicago wheat will have a natural rebound and may continue to rise, but there is unlikely to be a high rise. The Chicago and Winnipeg grain exchanges will be open until 1 PM next Monday.

River Rice Sales are Few as the Year Ends

(South Shanghai) Over 50 sources from various gangs (totaling over 8,000 piculs)

As the year-end approaches, money is tight, and people are unwilling to accumulate inventory. Sales of various goods are sparse. Prices of various thick japonica rices continue to fall by 1 to 2 jiao. Only the Weihaiwei gang bought about 200 bags of late rice, with prices falling by corners to over 1 jiao. At the same time, Du Yang pointed rice also fell by corners, only because of the shortage of Yin Bian Yuan Lai rice which was relatively stable.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, there were over 20 sources from various river wharves. In terms of sales, various colors remained sluggish. Only high-grade Bai Yuan rice was selling slowly. Market prices for high-grade Bai Geng rice were up small corners, while medium and lower grades were up smaller corners. Other sharp and early thin rice varieties were generally weak. Bai Yuan was stable.

Siam Broken Rice Falls by a Small Corner

Term Foreign Rice Continues to Transact

Yesterday, the demand for guest rice in this street was still good, and there was also some demand from the interior. However, with money being exceptionally tight at the end of the year, entry prices were generally low. And foreign wheat inventory was abundant, and foreign merchants were constantly seeking sales every day. Market sentiment remained flat and soft. There were many firm orders for Siam broken rice, and spot inventory was also abundant. Yesterday, only 2,000 bags were bought by the interior, and the price was immediately lowered by a small corner. Other rice varieties were able to stand firm with some effort because cargo owners insisted on their prices. The opening of 1,000 bags of West Guizhou rice was not affected and rose slightly. The inventory of Ke Xian from various routes has stabilized, but the speed of sales to the interior is slower than before. Market sentiment is also flat and soft. In general, there are few days left in the year. If there are no unexpected sales outlets, the market will not rise sharply. Term foreign rice continues to be sold by Dafu, with 500 tons of West grade for April being purchased by this street. Foreign merchants are very keen to sell, and there may be a large number of agreements reached within the year.

Sugar Market: Xin Chao Qing Falls by Five or Six Corners

Yesterday's sentiment in the sugar market stabilized. The association's benchmark price for No. 24 raw sugar was 18 yuan and 6 jiao and a half for ordinary spot goods, and 18 yuan and 7 jiao and a half for goods stored in this warehouse, with no rise or fall. No. 89 Dutch red sugar was 14 yuan and 2 jiao for high-grade goods, with over 500 bags transacted. Ordinary was 14 yuan. No. 1 white from this factory remained at 18 yuan. Xin Chao Qing turned weak due to increased arrivals. Hao Fang's rejection was ineffective, and 800 bags were offered yesterday. Ti Zhuang Qing was 12 yuan and 2 jiao, second grade was 12 yuan, Huang Gang Qing was 11 yuan and 8 jiao to 7 jiao, Ban Nan Qing was 11 yuan and 6 jiao, and Longgang Qing was 21 yuan and a half, down 5 to 6 jiao from the previous board. Xin Zhi Chi continued to arrive in 700 bags, with over 600 bags offered at 14 yuan and a half. The quality of the goods was higher than before, but it was still insufficient. Over 300 boxes of Ben Pian Qing were offered at a price of 10 yuan and 8 jiao and a half, down a small corner and a half from before.

North-South Goods: Wood Ear Weak but Recovering

Rebound of Three or Four Yuan

Wood ear recently increased significantly because land prices in the Han market rose by 3 to 4 yuan. Although sales here have not been smooth, market prices have also risen accordingly. For example, small package ears of aviation grade were previously priced at 92 to 3 yuan, but are now priced at 97 yuan. Assorted brands range from 92 to 3 yuan to 82 to 3 yuan. Both the Fujian and Guangdong gangs continue to buy.
